\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__elements_8h_source_l00850}00850 \textcolor{comment}{  /// A class for elements that solve the equations of solid mechanics,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__elements_8h_source_l00851}00851 \textcolor{comment}{  /// based on the principle of virtual displacements, with a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__elements_8h_source_l00852}00852 \textcolor{comment}{  /// contitutive equation that involves a pressure. This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__elements_8h_source_l00853}00853 \textcolor{comment}{  /// formulation is required in the case of incompressible materials, in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__elements_8h_source_l00854}00854 \textcolor{comment}{  /// which the additional constraint that volume must be conserved is applied.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__elements_8h_source_l00855}00855 \textcolor{comment}{  /// In this case, the Incompressible flag must be set to true. If the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__elements_8h_source_l00856}00856 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Incompressible flag is not set to true, we use the nearly-\/incompressible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__elements_8h_source_l00857}00857 \textcolor{comment}{  /// formulation of the constitutive equations.}}
